## post_dataforseo_dataforseo_labs_amazon_bulk_search_volume_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |

| `(operation)` | This endpoint will provide you with search volume values for a maximum of 1,000 keywords in one API request. Here search volume represents the approximate number of monthly searches for a keyword on Amazon. The returned results are specific to the `keywords`, `location`, and `language` parameters specified in a POST request. | Returns Amazon search volume for a batch of keywords in a single request, so you can size demand across many keywords at once for the given location and language. | 单次请求为一批关键词返回 Amazon 搜索量,便于在指定地区与语言下一次性衡量多个关键词的需求规模。 |
| `req.keywords` | target keywords required field UTF-8 encoding maximum number of keywords you can specify in this array: 1000; the keywords will be converted to lowercase format learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | Target keywords to process in one request; supplied in UTF-8 and converted to lowercase before matching. | 单次请求要处理的目标关键词;以 UTF-8 提供,匹配前会被统一转为小写。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of the location required field if don’t specify location_code you can receive the list of available locations with their location_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages; Note: this endpoint currently supports the following locations and languages only: Australia – 2036, en Austria – 2040, de Canada – 2124, en Egypt – 2818, ar France – 2250, fr Germany – 2276, de India – 2356, en Italy – 2380, it Mexico – 2484, es Netherlands – 2528, nl Saudi Arabia – 2682, ar Singapore – 2702, en Spain – 2724, es United Arab Emirates – 2784, ar United Kingdom – 2826, en United States – 2840, en example: United States | Geographic target given by its full location name; supply either this or location_code. Look up valid names via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以完整地区名称指定的地理目标;与 location_code 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | location code required field if don’t specify location_name you can receive the list of available locations with their location_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages; Note: this endpoint currently supports these locations and languages only; example: 2840 | Geographic target given by its numeric location code; supply either this or location_name. Look up valid codes via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以数字地区代码指定的地理目标;与 location_name 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效代码。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of the language required field if don’t specify language_code you can receive the list of available languages with their language_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages Note: this endpoint currently supports these locations and languages only; example: English | Target language given by its full name; supply either this or language_code. Look up valid names via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以完整名称指定的目标语言;与 language_code 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | language code required field if don’t specify language_name you can receive the list of available languages with their language_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages Note: this endpoint currently supports these locations and languages only; example: en | Target language given by its short code; supply either this or language_name. Look up valid codes via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以简码指定的目标语言;与 language_name 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效代码。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Free-form label you attach to the task so you can match it to its result later; echoed back in the response data object. | 你为任务附加的自定义标签,便于事后将任务与结果对应;会在响应的 data 对象中原样回传。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version that produced this response. | 生成本响应的 API 版本。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall status code for the response; inspect it before reading results and handle non-success codes accordingly. | 本响应的总体状态码;读取结果前应先检查,并对非成功状态码做相应处理。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message that accompanies the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Wall-clock time spent producing the response, in seconds. | 生成响应所耗费的时间,单位为秒。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Wall-clock time spent producing the response, in seconds. | 生成响应所耗费的时间,单位为秒。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of elements in this task's result array. | 本任务 result 数组中的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments of the endpoint that produced the task. | 生成该任务的接口 URL 路径分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters supplied in the request. | 对请求中所传参数的回传。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | List of all fields available for the filters and order_by parameters, grouped by the endpoint they apply to. | 可用于 filters 与 order_by 参数的全部字段列表,按其适用的接口分组。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.location_code` | location code in a POST array if there is no data, then the value is null | Location code echoed from the request; null when no data applies. | 从请求回传的地区代码;无对应数据时为 null。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.total_count` | total amount of results in our database relevant to your request | Total number of matching records in the database for this request, which may exceed the number returned. | 数据库中匹配本请求的记录总数,可能多于实际返回的条数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items_count` | the number of results returned in the items array | Number of records returned in this items array. | 本 items 数组中返回的记录数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items` | contains keyword search volume data data | Returned records carrying the core data of this endpoint. | 返回的记录,承载本接口的核心数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |

## post_dataforseo_dataforseo_labs_amazon_product_keyword_intersections_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |

| `(operation)` | This endpoint will provide you with a list of keywords for which the target products intersect in Amazon SERP. The returned results are specific to the `asins` specified in a POST request. Learn more about ASIN in [this help center article.](https://dataforseo.com/help-center/asin-in-amazon-api) | Returns the keywords for which the supplied Amazon products appear together in the same SERP, along with each product's SERP element per keyword, revealing where multiple ASINs compete or co-rank. | 返回所传 Amazon 商品在同一 SERP 中共同出现的关键词,并给出每个关键词下各商品的 SERP 元素,揭示多个 ASIN 在何处竞争或同台排名。 |
| `req.asins` | asins of target products required field product IDs of the products for which you need to find keyword intersections; specify the ASINs as in the following example: "asins": { "1": "019005476X", "2": "0190074442" } the maximum number of ASINs you can specify in this object is 20; learn more about the parameter on this help center page | Target products' ASINs to pull ranking data for in one batch; obtain each ASIN from the Amazon Products endpoint and supply them in uppercase. | 需批量获取排名数据的目标商品 ASIN 列表;每个 ASIN 可从 Amazon Products 接口获取,需以大写形式提供。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of the location required field if don’t specify location_code you can receive the list of available locations with their location_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages; Note: this endpoint currently supports the US, Egypt, Saudi Arabia, and the United Arab Emirates locations only; example: United Kingdom | Geographic target given by its full location name; supply either this or location_code. Look up valid names via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以完整地区名称指定的地理目标;与 location_code 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | location code required field if don’t specify location_name you can receive the list of available locations with their location_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages; Note: this endpoint currently supports the US, Egypt, Saudi Arabia, and the United Arab Emirates locations only; example: 2840 | Geographic target given by its numeric location code; supply either this or location_name. Look up valid codes via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以数字地区代码指定的地理目标;与 location_name 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效代码。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of the language required field if don’t specify language_code you can receive the list of available languages with their language_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages example: English | Target language given by its full name; supply either this or language_code. Look up valid names via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以完整名称指定的目标语言;与 language_code 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | language code required field if don’t specify language_name you can receive the list of available languages with their language_code by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages example: en | Target language given by its short code; supply either this or language_name. Look up valid codes via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以简码指定的目标语言;与 language_name 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效代码。 |
| `req.limit` | the maximum number of products in the results array optional field default value: 100; maximum value: 1000 | Caps how many records are returned in the results array. | 限定 results 数组中返回的记录条数上限。 |
| `req.intersection_mode` | mode for finding asin intersections optional field possible values: union, intersect; default value: intersect; learn more about the parameter in this help center guide | How the supplied ASINs are matched against keywords: intersect keeps only keywords where every ASIN co-ranks, while union keeps keywords where any of them ranks. | 所传 ASIN 与关键词的匹配方式:intersect 仅保留全部 ASIN 同台排名的关键词,union 则保留其中任一 ASIN 有排名的关键词。 |
| `req.filters` | array of results filtering parameters optional field you can add several filters at once (8 filters maximum) you should set a logical operator and, or between the conditions the following operators are supported: regex, not_regex, , , >, >=, =, , in, not_in, ilike, not_ilike, like, not_like, match, not_match you can use the % operator with like and not_like, as well as ilike and not_ilike to match any string of zero or more characters example: ["avg_position"," for more information about filters, please refer to Dataforseo Labs – Filters or this help center guide | Conditions that narrow the result set; combine clauses with the and / or logical operators. Reference fields by their response dotpath (e.g. metrics.organic.pos_1).<br>[⚠️Note:源码描述的运算符与最大条件数在各接口间不一致且部分符号被渲染截断，具体可用运算符与上限请以原生 description 为准，待研发确认。] | 用于收窄结果集的筛选条件;子句之间以 and / or 逻辑运算符组合。字段以其响应点路径引用(如 metrics.organic.pos_1)。<br>[⚠️批注:源码描述的运算符与最大条件数在各接口间不一致且部分符号被渲染截断，具体可用运算符与上限请以原生 description 为准，待研发确认。] |
| `req.order_by` | results sorting rules optional field you can use the same values as in the filters array to sort the results possible sorting types: asc – results will be sorted in the ascending order desc – results will be sorted in the descending order you should use a comma to set up a sorting parameter example: ["sum_position,desc"] note that you can set no more than three sorting rules in a single request you should use a comma to separate several sorting rules example: ["intersections,desc","avg_position,asc"] default rule: ["intersections,desc"] | Sorting rules over the same fields usable in filters; each rule pairs a field with an asc or desc direction. | 针对 filters 中可用字段的排序规则;每条规则将一个字段与 asc 或 desc 方向配对。 |
| `req.offset` | offset in the results array of returned keywords optional field default value: 0 if you specify the 10 value, the first ten keywords in the results array will be omitted and the data will be provided for the successive keywords | Skips this many leading records in the results array, for paging through results. | 跳过 results 数组开头的指定条数记录,用于分页浏览结果。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result` | data on the intersection | Per-app SERP data for the returned keyword, with one array per supplied app ID. | 返回关键词的逐应用 SERP 数据,每个传入应用 ID 对应一个数组。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number` | intersection data for one of the ASINs in a POST request | The Amazon SERP element for one of the supplied ASINs; the key name is that product's ASIN. | 对应某一个传入 ASIN 的 Amazon SERP 元素;键名即该商品的 ASIN。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.type` | type of element = ‘amazon_serp’ | Type of the SERP element. | SERP 元素的类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.rank_group` | position within a group of elements with identical type values positions of elements with different type values are omitted from rank_group | Rank within the group of elements sharing the same type; other types are skipped in this count. | 在同类型元素组内的排名;其他类型不计入该计数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.rank_absolute` | absolute rank in Amazon SERP absolute position among all the elements in SERP | Absolute rank of the element among all elements in the SERP. | 该元素在整个 SERP 全部元素中的绝对排名。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.position` | the alignment of the element in Amazon SERP can take the following values: left, right | Horizontal alignment of the product element within the SERP (left or right). | 商品元素在 SERP 中的水平对齐方位(left 或 right)。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.xpath` | the XPath of the element | XPath pointing to the product element within the SERP page markup. | 指向该商品元素在 SERP 页面标记中位置的 XPath。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.domain` | Amazon domain | Amazon domain the product was found on. | 检出该商品所在的 Amazon 域名。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.title` | product title | Title of the product. | 商品的标题。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.url` | URL of the product page | URL of the product's Amazon page. | 商品 Amazon 页面的 URL。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.description` | description of the product | Product description text from the Amazon listing. | Amazon Listing 的商品描述文本。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.asin` | ASIN of the product learn more about ASIN in this help center guide | Product ASIN; in results, the ASIN this record describes. | 商品 ASIN;在结果中为该记录所描述的 ASIN。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.image_url` | URL of the product image featured in the results | URL of the product's image in the listing. | Listing 中商品图片的 URL。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.price_from` | the regular price of a product example: 49.98 | Lower bound of the product's price range shown in the listing. | Listing 中商品价格区间的下限。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.price_to` | the upper limit of the product price range example: 384.99 | Upper bound of the product's price range shown in the listing. | Listing 中商品价格区间的上限。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.currency` | currency in the ISO format example: USD | ISO currency code applied to the listed price. | Listing 价格所用的 ISO 货币代码。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.special_offers` | special offer details contains special offer details, including coupon and Subscribe & Save discounts | Special offers or promotions listed for the product. | 该商品列出的特价或促销信息。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.is_best_seller` | “Best Seller” label if the value is true, the product is marked with the “Best Seller” label | Whether the listing carries Amazon's “Best Seller” badge. | 该 Listing 是否带有 Amazon “Best Seller” 标识。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.is_amazon_choice` | “Amazon’s choice” label if the value is true, the product is marked with the “Amazon’s choice” label | Whether the listing carries Amazon's “Amazon's Choice” badge. | 该 Listing 是否带有 Amazon “Amazon's Choice” 标识。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.rating` | the item’s rating the popularity rate based on reviews and displayed in SERP | Average customer rating of the product. | 商品的平均用户评分。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.rating.rating_type` | the type of rating here you can find the following elements: Max5, Percents, CustomMax | Rating scale used; Max5 denotes a 0-5 scale. | 所用评分量表;Max5 表示 0 至 5 分制。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.rating.value` | the value of the rating | The rating value. | 评分数值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.rating.votes_count` | the amount of feedback | Number of ratings contributing to the value. | 参与构成该评分的评价数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.rating.rating_max` | the maximum value for a rating_type | Maximum possible value for the rating scale. | 该评分量表的最大可能值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.delivery_info` | delivery information delivery information including free and fast delivery date ranges | Delivery details for the product, including the delivery message and price. | 商品的配送信息,包含配送说明与配送价格。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.delivery_info.delivery_message` | delivery information message accompanying the delivery information as posted by the seller | Delivery message shown in the listing (e.g. estimated arrival). | Listing 中显示的配送说明(如预计送达)。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.delivery_info.delivery_price` | price for the delivery price of the delivery based on the location you specified in the POST request; if free delivery is available, the value is null | Delivery price details for the product. | 商品的配送价格详情。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.delivery_info.delivery_price.current` | current delivery price | Current price shown in the listing. | Listing 中显示的当前价格。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.delivery_info.delivery_price.regular` | regular undiscounted delivery price | Regular (non-promotional) price shown in the listing. | Listing 中显示的常规(非促销)价格。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.delivery_info.delivery_price.max_value` | maximum undiscounted delivery price | Maximum price shown in the listing. | Listing 中显示的最高价格。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.delivery_info.delivery_price.currency` | currency in the ISO format | ISO currency code applied to the listed price. | Listing 价格所用的 ISO 货币代码。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.delivery_info.delivery_price.is_price_range` | indicates whether the delivery price is a range | Whether the price is given as a range rather than a single value. | 价格是否以区间而非单一数值给出。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.$asin_number.delivery_info.delivery_price.displayed_price` | price line provided as displayed in Amazon listing | Raw price string exactly as shown in the listing. | Listing 中原样展示的价格字符串。 |

## post_dataforseo_dataforseo_labs_amazon_ranked_keywords_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | This endpoint will provide you with a list of keywords the target product ranks for on Amazon. The returned results are specific to the `asin` specified in a POST request. Learn more about ASIN in [this help center article.](https://dataforseo.com/help-center/asin-in-amazon-api) | Returns the keywords a target ASIN ranks for in Amazon SERPs, each with keyword metrics and the product's ranking SERP element, for the given location and language. | 返回目标 ASIN 在 Amazon SERP 中有排名的关键词,每个关键词附带关键词指标及该商品的排名 SERP 元素,按指定地区与语言限定。 |
| `req.asin` | product ID required field unique product identifier (ASIN) on Amazon; you can receive the asin parameter by making a separate request to the Amazon Products endpoint | Target product's Amazon ASIN; competitors are computed relative to this listing. Obtain it from the Amazon Products endpoint. | 目标商品的 Amazon ASIN,竞品以此 Listing 为基准计算。可从 Amazon Products 接口获取。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of the location required field if don’t specify location_code you can receive the list of available locations with their location_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages; Note: this endpoint currently supports the US, Egypt, Saudi Arabia, and the United Arab Emirates locations only; example: United States | Geographic target given by its full location name; supply either this or location_code. Look up valid names via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以完整地区名称指定的地理目标;与 location_code 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | location code required field if don’t specify location_name you can receive the list of available locations with their location_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages; Note: this endpoint currently supports the US, Egypt, Saudi Arabia, and the United Arab Emirates locations only; example: 2840 | Geographic target given by its numeric location code; supply either this or location_name. Look up valid codes via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以数字地区代码指定的地理目标;与 location_name 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效代码。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of the language required field if don’t specify language_code you can receive the list of available languages with their language_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages example: English | Target language given by its full name; supply either this or language_code. Look up valid names via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以完整名称指定的目标语言;与 language_code 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | language code required field if don’t specify language_name you can receive the list of available languages with their language_code by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages example: en | Target language given by its short code; supply either this or language_name. Look up valid codes via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以简码指定的目标语言;与 language_name 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效代码。 |
| `req.limit` | the maximum number of products in the results array optional field default value: 100; maximum value: 1000 | Caps how many records are returned in the results array. | 限定 results 数组中返回的记录条数上限。 |
| `req.ignore_synonyms` | ignore highly similar keywords optional field if set to true only core keywords will be returned, all highly similar keywords will be excluded; default value: false | When true, collapses highly similar keywords and returns only the core keyword of each cluster. | 为 true 时,合并高度相似的关键词,每个簇仅返回核心关键词。 |
| `req.filters` | array of results filtering parameters optional field you can add several filters at once (8 filters maximum) you should set a logical operator and, or between the conditions the following operators are supported: regex, not_regex, , , >, >=, =, , in, not_in, like, not_like, match, not_match you can use the % operator with like and not_like to match any string of zero or more characters example: ["keyword_data.keyword_info.search_volume","in",[100,1000]]; for more information about filters, please refer to Dataforseo Labs – Filters or this help center guide | Conditions that narrow the result set; combine clauses with the and / or logical operators. Reference fields by their response dotpath (e.g. metrics.organic.pos_1).<br>[⚠️Note:源码描述的运算符与最大条件数在各接口间不一致且部分符号被渲染截断，具体可用运算符与上限请以原生 description 为准，待研发确认。] | 用于收窄结果集的筛选条件;子句之间以 and / or 逻辑运算符组合。字段以其响应点路径引用(如 metrics.organic.pos_1)。<br>[⚠️批注:源码描述的运算符与最大条件数在各接口间不一致且部分符号被渲染截断，具体可用运算符与上限请以原生 description 为准，待研发确认。] |
| `req.order_by` | results sorting rules optional field you can use the same values as in the filters array to sort the results possible sorting types: asc – results will be sorted in the ascending order desc – results will be sorted in the descending order you should use a comma to set up a sorting parameter example: ["keyword_data.keyword_info.competition,desc"] default rule: ["ranked_serp_element.serp_item.rank_group,asc"] note that you can set no more than three sorting rules in a single request you should use a comma to separate several sorting rules example: ["keyword_data.keyword_info.search_volume,desc","keyword_data.keyword_info.cpc,desc"] | Sorting rules over the same fields usable in filters; each rule pairs a field with an asc or desc direction. | 针对 filters 中可用字段的排序规则;每条规则将一个字段与 asc 或 desc 方向配对。 |
| `req.offset` | offset in the results array of returned keywords optional field default value: 0 if you specify the 10 value, the first ten keywords in the results array will be omitted and the data will be provided for the successive keywords | Skips this many leading records in the results array, for paging through results. | 跳过 results 数组开头的指定条数记录,用于分页浏览结果。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Free-form label you attach to the task so you can match it to its result later; echoed back in the response data object. | 你为任务附加的自定义标签,便于事后将任务与结果对应;会在响应的 data 对象中原样回传。 |

## post_dataforseo_dataforseo_labs_apple_app_competitors_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |

| `(operation)` | This endpoint will provide you with a list of mobile applications that intersect with the target app for its ranking keywords on App Store. You will obtain the IDs of competitor apps along with search volume and ranking data on competitor ranking keywords. | Returns the apps that compete with a target App Store app across its ranking keywords, including each competitor's app ID and ranking metrics over the shared keywords. | 返回在 App Store 上与目标应用争夺相同排名关键词的竞品应用,包含各竞品的应用 ID 及在共有关键词上的排名指标。 |
| `req.app_id` | id of the app required field ID of the mobile application on App Store; you can find the ID in the URL of every app listed on App Store; example: in the URL https://apps.apple.com/us/app/id835599320 the id is 835599320 | Target mobile app's store ID, taken from the app's store URL; results cover the keywords this app ranks for. | 目标移动应用的商店 ID,取自应用商店页 URL;结果覆盖该应用所排名的关键词。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of the location required field if you don’t specify location_code Note: it is required to specify either location_name or location_code you can receive the list of available locations with their location_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages; Note: this endpoint currently supports the US location only; example: United States | Geographic target given by its full location name; supply either this or location_code. Look up valid names via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以完整地区名称指定的地理目标;与 location_code 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | location code required field if you don’t specify location_name Note: it is required to specify either location_name or location_code you can receive the list of available locations with their location_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages; Note: this endpoint currently supports the US location only; example: 2840 | Geographic target given by its numeric location code; supply either this or location_name. Look up valid codes via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以数字地区代码指定的地理目标;与 location_name 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效代码。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of the language required field if you don’t specify language_code Note: it is required to specify either language_name or language_code you can receive the list of available languages with their language_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages; Note: this endpoint currently supports the English language only; example: English | Target language given by its full name; supply either this or language_code. Look up valid names via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以完整名称指定的目标语言;与 language_code 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | language code required field if you don’t specify language_name Note: it is required to specify either language_name or language_code you can receive the list of available languages with their language_code by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages; Note: this endpoint currently supports the English language only example: en | Target language given by its short code; supply either this or language_name. Look up valid codes via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以简码指定的目标语言;与 language_name 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效代码。 |
| `req.filters` | array of results filtering parameters optional field you can add several filters at once (8 filters maximum) you should set a logical operator and, or between the conditions the following operators are supported: , , >, >=, =, , in, not_in example: ["intersections",">",500] [["competitor_metrics.app_store_search_organic.pos_1","",10],"and",["avg_position",">=","10"]] [[["intersections",">=",50],"and",["competitor_metrics.app_store_search_organic.pos_1","in",[1,5]]], "or", ["sum_position",">=","10000"]] for more information about filters, please refer to Dataforseo Labs – Filters or this help center guide | Conditions that narrow the result set; combine clauses with the and / or logical operators. Reference fields by their response dotpath (e.g. metrics.organic.pos_1).<br>[⚠️Note:源码描述的运算符与最大条件数在各接口间不一致且部分符号被渲染截断，具体可用运算符与上限请以原生 description 为准，待研发确认。] | 用于收窄结果集的筛选条件;子句之间以 and / or 逻辑运算符组合。字段以其响应点路径引用(如 metrics.organic.pos_1)。<br>[⚠️批注:源码描述的运算符与最大条件数在各接口间不一致且部分符号被渲染截断，具体可用运算符与上限请以原生 description 为准，待研发确认。] |
| `req.order_by` | results sorting rules optional field you can use the same values as in the filters array to sort the results; possible sorting types: asc – results will be sorted in the ascending order; desc – results will be sorted in the descending order; you should use a comma to specify a sorting type; example: ["intersections,asc"] Note: you can set no more than three sorting rules in a single request; you should use a comma to separate several sorting rules; example: ["intersections,desc","sum_position,asc"] default rule: ["intersections,desc"] Note: if the item_types array contains item types that are different from organic, the results will be ordered by the first item type in the array | Sorting rules over the same fields usable in filters; each rule pairs a field with an asc or desc direction. | 针对 filters 中可用字段的排序规则;每条规则将一个字段与 asc 或 desc 方向配对。 |
| `req.limit` | the maximum number of returned apps optional field default value: 100 maximum value: 1000 | Caps how many records are returned in the results array. | 限定 results 数组中返回的记录条数上限。 |
| `req.offset` | offset in the results array of returned apps optional field default value: 0 if you specify the 10 value, the first ten apps in the results array will be omitted and the data will be provided for the successive keywords | Skips this many leading records in the results array, for paging through results. | 跳过 results 数组开头的指定条数记录,用于分页浏览结果。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Free-form label you attach to the task so you can match it to its result later; echoed back in the response data object. | 你为任务附加的自定义标签,便于事后将任务与结果对应;会在响应的 data 对象中原样回传。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.items_count` | the number of results returned in the items array | Number of records returned in this items array. | 本 items 数组中返回的记录数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items` | contains data related to the app_id and competitor applications | Returned records carrying the core data of this endpoint. | 返回的记录,承载本接口的核心数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.app_id` | id of the competitor app | App store ID; in results, the app this record describes. | 应用商店 ID;在结果中为该记录所描述的应用。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.avg_position` | average position of the app in App Store SERP Note: average position is calculated for intersected keywords only; the value for a given application may differ when combined with different target applications | Average SERP position of the entity across the matched keywords. | 实体在匹配关键词上的平均 SERP 排名位置。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.sum_position` | sum of all app positions in App Store SERP Note: sum position is calculated for intersected keywords only; the value for a given application may differ when combined with different target applications | Sum of the entity's positions across the intersected keywords. | 实体在交集关键词上各排名位置之和。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersections` | number of intersecting keywords | Number of keywords the entity shares with the target. | 实体与目标共有的关键词数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.competitor_metrics` | metrics for intersecting keywords ranking data relevant to the keywords that the provided competitor application shares with the app in a POST request; note: in this array ranking data is provided for the returned competitor’s app_id | Ranking metrics over the keywords this competitor shares with the target. | 该竞争方与目标共有关键词上的排名指标。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.competitor_metrics.app_store_search_organic` | ranking data from App Store organic search | Ranking data from App Store organic search. | 来自 App Store 自然搜索的排名数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.competitor_metrics.app_store_search_organic.pos_1` | number of SERPs where the competitor app ranks #1 in organic results | Count of SERPs where the entity ranks #1. | 实体排名第 1 的 SERP 数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.competitor_metrics.app_store_search_organic.pos_2_3` | number of SERPs where the competitor app ranks #2-3 in organic results | Count of SERPs where the entity ranks in positions 2-3. | 实体排名第 2 至 3 位的 SERP 数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.competitor_metrics.app_store_search_organic.pos_4_10` | number of SERPs where the competitor app ranks #4-10 in organic results | Count of SERPs where the entity ranks in positions 4-10. | 实体排名第 4 至 10 位的 SERP 数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.competitor_metrics.app_store_search_organic.pos_11_100` | number of SERPs where the competitor app ranks #11-100 in organic results | Count of SERPs where the entity ranks in positions 11-100. | 实体排名第 11 至 100 位的 SERP 数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.competitor_metrics.app_store_search_organic.count` | total count of organic SERPs that contain the competitor app | Total count of SERPs of this type that contain the entity. | 包含该实体的此类 SERP 总数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.competitor_metrics.app_store_search_organic.search_volume` | total search volume of the intersecting keywords in App Store organic SERP | Approximate average monthly search volume for the keyword. | 关键词的近似月均搜索量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.full_metrics` | metrics for all keywords of the application full overview of ranking data relevant to all keywords that the provided app_id is ranking for | Ranking metrics over all keywords this entity ranks for, not just the shared ones. | 该主体所有排名关键词(而非仅共有关键词)上的排名指标。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.full_metrics.app_store_search_organic` | ranking data from App Store organic search | Ranking data from App Store organic search. | 来自 App Store 自然搜索的排名数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.full_metrics.app_store_search_organic.pos_1` | number of SERPs where the competitor app ranks #1 in organic results | Count of SERPs where the entity ranks #1. | 实体排名第 1 的 SERP 数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.full_metrics.app_store_search_organic.pos_2_3` | number of SERPs where the competitor app ranks #2-3 in organic results | Count of SERPs where the entity ranks in positions 2-3. | 实体排名第 2 至 3 位的 SERP 数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.full_metrics.app_store_search_organic.pos_4_10` | number of SERPs where the competitor app ranks #4-10 in organic results | Count of SERPs where the entity ranks in positions 4-10. | 实体排名第 4 至 10 位的 SERP 数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.full_metrics.app_store_search_organic.pos_11_100` | number of SERPs where the competitor app ranks #11-100 in organic results | Count of SERPs where the entity ranks in positions 11-100. | 实体排名第 11 至 100 位的 SERP 数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.full_metrics.app_store_search_organic.count` | total count of organic SERPs that contain the competitor app | Total count of SERPs of this type that contain the entity. | 包含该实体的此类 SERP 总数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.full_metrics.app_store_search_organic.search_volume` | total search volume of the app’s ranking keywords in App Store organic SERP | Approximate average monthly search volume for the keyword. | 关键词的近似月均搜索量。 |

## post_dataforseo_dataforseo_labs_google_app_intersection_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | This endpoint will provide you with a list of keywords for which the mobile applications specified in the `app_ids` object rank within the same Google Play SERP. | Returns the keywords for which several Google Play apps appear together in the same SERP, revealing the keyword overlap among the apps you supply in app_ids. | 返回多个 Google Play 应用在同一 SERP 中共同出现的关键词,揭示 app_ids 中所列应用之间的关键词重叠。 |
| `req.app_ids` | ids of the target apps required field IDs of the target mobile applications on Google Play; you can find the ID in the URL of every app listed on Google Play; example: in the URL https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=org.telegram.messenger the id is org.telegram.messenger;; the ids should be specified the following way: "app_ids": { "1": "org.telegram.messenger", "2": "com.zhiliaoapp.musically" } if you specify a single ID here, the API will return results only for one application; the maximum number of app IDs you can specify in this object is 20 | IDs of the target apps whose keyword overlap you want; take each ID from the app's App Store URL and supply them as an object of indexed entries. | 需求取关键词交集的目标应用 ID;每个 ID 取自 App Store 页 URL,以带序号条目的对象形式提供。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of the location required field if you don’t specify location_code Note: it is required to specify either location_name or location_code you can receive the list of available locations with their location_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages; Note: this endpoint currently supports the US location only; example: United States | Geographic target given by its full location name; supply either this or location_code. Look up valid names via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以完整地区名称指定的地理目标;与 location_code 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效名称。 |

| `req.language_name` | full name of the language required field if you don’t specify language_code Note: it is required to specify either language_name or language_code you can receive the list of available languages with their language_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages; Note: this endpoint currently supports the English language only; example: English | Target language given by its full name; supply either this or language_code. Look up valid codes via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以简码指定的目标语言;与 language_name 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效代码。 |
| `req.filters` | array of results filtering parameters optional field you can add several filters at once (8 filters maximum) you should set a logical operator and, or between the conditions the following operators are supported: , , >, >=, =, , in, not_in example: ["keyword_data.keyword_info.search_volume",">",500] [["keyword_data.keyword_info.search_volume","",500],"and",[intersection_result.382617920.rank_group",">=","10"]] for more information about filters, please refer to Dataforseo Labs – Filters or this help center guide | Conditions that narrow the result set; combine clauses with the and / or logical operators. Reference fields by their response dotpath (e.g. metrics.organic.pos_1).<br>[⚠️Note:源码描述的运算符与最大条件数在各接口间不一致且部分符号被渲染截断，具体可用运算符与上限请以原生 description 为准，待研发确认。] | 用于收窄结果集的筛选条件;子句之间以 and / or 逻辑运算符组合。字段以其响应点路径引用(如 metrics.organic.pos_1)。<br>[⚠️批注:源码描述的运算符与最大条件数在各接口间不一致且部分符号被渲染截断，具体可用运算符与上限请以原生 description 为准，待研发确认。] |
| `req.order_by` | results sorting rules optional field you can use the same values as in the filters array to sort the results; possible sorting types: asc – results will be sorted in the ascending order; desc – results will be sorted in the descending order; you should use a comma to specify a sorting type; example: ["intersection_result.382617920.rank_absolute,asc"] Note: you can set no more than three sorting rules in a single request; you should use a comma to separate several sorting rules; example: ["intersection_result.382617920.rank_absolute,desc","keyword_data.keyword_info.search_volume,asc"] default rule: ["keyword_data.keyword_info.search_volume,desc"] Note: if the item_types array contains item types that are different from organic, the results will be ordered by the first item type in the array | Sorting rules over the same fields usable in filters; each rule pairs a field with an asc or desc direction. | 针对 filters 中可用字段的排序规则;每条规则将一个字段与 asc 或 desc 方向配对。 |
| `req.limit` | the maximum number of returned keywords optional field default value: 100 maximum value: 1000 | Caps how many records are returned in the results array. | 限定 results 数组中返回的记录条数上限。 |
| `req.offset` | offset in the results array of returned keywords optional field default value: 0 if you specify the 10 value, the first ten keywords in the results array will be omitted and the data will be provided for the successive keywords | Skips this many leading records in the results array, for paging through results. | 跳过 results 数组开头的指定条数记录,用于分页浏览结果。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Free-form label you attach to the task so you can match it to its result later; echoed back in the response data object. | 你为任务附加的自定义标签,便于事后将任务与结果对应;会在响应的 data 对象中原样回传。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version that produced this response. | 生成本响应的 API 版本。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall status code for the response; inspect it before reading results and handle non-success codes accordingly. | 本响应的总体状态码;读取结果前应先检查,并对非成功状态码做相应处理。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message that accompanies the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Wall-clock time spent producing the response, in seconds. | 生成响应所耗费的时间,单位为秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total charge for all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本响应中所有任务的合计费用,单位为美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task objects in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中任务对象的数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | Number of tasks in the tasks array that returned an error. | tasks 数组中以错误返回的任务数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task objects, one per task in the request batch. | 任务对象列表,请求批次中每个任务对应一项。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique task identifier in UUID format. | 任务在系统中的唯一标识,采用 UUID 格式。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of the response codes here | Overall status code for the response; inspect it before reading results and handle non-success codes accordingly. | 本响应的总体状态码;读取结果前应先检查,并对非成功状态码做相应处理。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message that accompanies the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Wall-clock time spent producing the response, in seconds. | 生成响应所耗费的时间,单位为秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Total charge for all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本响应中所有任务的合计费用,单位为美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of elements in this task's result array. | 本任务 result 数组中的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments of the endpoint that produced the task. | 生成该任务的接口 URL 路径分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters supplied in the request. | 对请求中所传参数的回传。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | List of all fields available for the filters and order_by parameters, grouped by the endpoint they apply to. | 可用于 filters 与 order_by 参数的全部字段列表,按其适用的接口分组。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.app_ids` | ids of the apps in a POST array | App IDs echoed from the request. | 从请求回传的应用 ID。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.location_code` | location code in a POST array | Location code echoed from the request; null when no data applies. | 从请求回传的地区代码;无对应数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.language_code` | language code in a POST array | Language code echoed from the request; null when no data applies. | 从请求回传的语言代码;无对应数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.total_count` | total amount of results in our database relevant to your request | Total number of matching records in the database for this request, which may exceed the number returned. | 数据库中匹配本请求的记录总数,可能多于实际返回的条数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items_count` | the number of results returned in the items array | Number of records returned in this items array. | 本 items 数组中返回的记录数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items` | contains data related to the ranking keywords for the app specified in the app_id field | Returned records carrying the core data of this endpoint. | 返回的记录,承载本接口的核心数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data` | keyword data for the returned keyword | Keyword metrics and SERP data for the returned keyword. | 返回关键词的指标与 SERP 数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.keyword` | returned keyword | The keyword this record describes. | 该记录所描述的关键词。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.location_code` | location code in a POST array | Location code echoed from the request; null when no data applies. | 从请求回传的地区代码;无对应数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.language_code` | language code in a POST array | Language code echoed from the request; null when no data applies. | 从请求回传的语言代码;无对应数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.keyword_info` | keyword info for the returned keyword | Core keyword metrics block (volume, competition, bids, categories, and history). | 核心关键词指标块(搜索量、竞争度、出价、类目与历史)。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.keyword_info.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.keyword_info.last_updated_time` | date and time when keyword data was updated in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00”; example: 2019-11-15 12:57:46 +00:00 | When this data was last refreshed, in UTC (“yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00”). | 该数据最近一次刷新的时间,UTC 格式(“yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00”)。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.keyword_info.competition` | competition represents the relative amount of competition associated with the given keyword; the value is based on Google Ads data and can be between 0 and 1 (inclusive); in this case, will equal null | Relative amount of paid competition for the keyword, derived from Google Ads data on a 0-to-1 scale. | 关键词的相对付费竞争程度,基于 Google Ads 数据,取值范围 0 至 1。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.keyword_info.competition_level` | competition level represents the relative level of competition associated with the given keyword in paid SERP only; possible values: LOW, MEDIUM, HIGH if competition level is unknown, the value is null; learn more about the metric in this help center article; in this case, will equal null | Bucketed paid-competition level for the keyword; LOW, MEDIUM, and HIGH denote increasing competition, and an unknown level is null. | 关键词付费竞争的分档:LOW、MEDIUM、HIGH 依次表示竞争由低到高,未知时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.keyword_info.cpc` | cost-per-click represents the average cost per click (USD) historically paid for the keyword; in this case, will equal null | Average historical cost per click for the keyword, in USD. | 关键词历史平均的单次点击成本,单位为美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.keyword_info.search_volume` | average monthly search volume rate represents the (approximate) number of searches for the given keyword on Google Play | Approximate average monthly search volume for the keyword. | 关键词的近似月均搜索量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.keyword_info.low_top_of_page_bid` | minimum bid for the ad to be displayed at the top of the first page indicates the value greater than about 20% of the lowest bids for which ads were displayed (based on Google Ads statistics for advertisers) the value may differ depending on the location specified in a POST request; in this case, will equal null | Lower-end top-of-page bid estimate (around the 20th percentile of winning bids), varying by the requested location. | 页首广告出价的低端估计(约为中标出价的 20 分位),随请求地区而变。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.keyword_info.high_top_of_page_bid` | maximum bid for the ad to be displayed at the top of the first page indicates the value greater than about 80% of the lowest bids for which ads were displayed (based on Google Ads statistics for advertisers) the value may differ depending on the location specified in a POST request; in this case, will equal null | Upper-end top-of-page bid estimate (around the 80th percentile of winning bids), varying by the requested location. | 页首广告出价的高端估计(约为中标出价的 80 分位),随请求地区而变。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.keyword_info.categories` | product and service categories you can download the full list of possible categories; in this case, will equal null | Product and service category IDs the keyword belongs to; the full category list is downloadable from DataForSEO. | 关键词所属的产品与服务类目 ID;完整类目清单可从 DataForSEO 下载。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.keyword_info.monthly_searches` | monthly searches represents the (approximate) number of searches for this keyword (as available for the past twelve months), targeted to the specified geographic locations; in this case, will equal null | Per-month search volume history for roughly the trailing twelve months. | 约近 12 个月的逐月搜索量历史。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.serp_info` | SERP data the value will be null if you didn’t set the field include_serp_info to true in the POST array or if there is no SERP data for this keyword in our database | SERP-level data for the keyword; null unless include_serp_info was set and SERP data exists for the keyword. | 关键词的 SERP 级数据;除非设置了 include_serp_info 且数据库存有该关键词的 SERP 数据,否则为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.serp_info.se_type` | search engine type search engine type specified in a POST request; for this endpoint, the field equals bing | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.serp_info.check_url` | direct URL to search engine results you can use it to make sure that we provided accurate results | Direct URL to the live search results, usable to verify the returned data. | 指向实时搜索结果的直达 URL,可用于核对返回数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.serp_info.serp_item_types` | types of search results in SERP contains types of search results (items) found in SERP; in this case, will equal null | The kinds of SERP features (items) found in the results for this keyword. | 该关键词结果中出现的 SERP 功能(item)类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.serp_info.se_results_count` | number of search results for the returned keyword | Number of search results the engine reports for the keyword. | 搜索引擎为该关键词报告的搜索结果数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.serp_info.last_updated_time` | date and time when SERP data was updated in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00” example: 2019-11-15 12:57:46 +00:00 | When this data was last refreshed, in UTC (“yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00”). | 该数据最近一次刷新的时间,UTC 格式(“yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00”)。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.serp_info.previous_updated_time` | previous to the most recent date and time when SERP data was updated in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00” example: 2019-10-15 12:57:46 +00:00 | When this data was refreshed prior to the most recent update, in UTC. | 该数据在最近一次更新之前的刷新时间,UTC 格式。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result` | contains SERP data for the returned keyword data will be provided in separate arrays for each app ID you specified in the app_ids object when setting a task; depending on the number of specified app IDs, it can contain from 1 to 20 arrays named respectively | Per-app SERP data for the returned keyword, with one array per supplied app ID. | 返回关键词的逐应用 SERP 数据,每个传入应用 ID 对应一个数组。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.1` | contains SERP data for the respective app ID field name varies in the range from 1 to 20 according to the number of app IDs in the app_ids object; possible types of SERP elements: google_play_search_organic | SERP elements for one of the supplied app IDs; the key name varies from 1 to the number of app IDs you provided in app_ids. | 对应某一个传入应用 ID 的 SERP 元素;键名从 1 起,按 app_ids 中提供的应用 ID 数量递增。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.1.type` | type of the SERP element possible values: google_play_search_organic | Type of the SERP element. | SERP 元素的类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.1.rank_group` | position within a group of elements with identical type values positions of elements with different type values are omitted from rank_group | Rank within the group of elements sharing the same type; other types are skipped in this count. | 在同类型元素组内的排名;其他类型不计入该计数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.1.rank_absolute` | absolute rank in SERP absolute position among all the elements in SERP | Absolute rank of the element among all elements in the SERP. | 该元素在整个 SERP 全部元素中的绝对排名。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.1.position` | the alignment of the element in SERP can take the following values: left, right | Horizontal alignment of the element within the SERP (left or right). | 元素在 SERP 中的水平对齐方位(left 或 right)。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.1.app_id` | id of the app | App store ID; in results, the app this record describes. | 应用商店 ID;在结果中为该记录所描述的应用。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.1.title` | title of the app | Title of the app. | 应用的标题。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.1.url` | URL to the app page on Google Play | URL of the app's store page. | 应用商店页的 URL。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.1.icon` | URL to the app icon | URL of the app icon. | 应用图标的 URL。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.1.reviews_count` | the total number of reviews of the app | Total number of reviews the app has. | 应用的评价总数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.1.rating` | average rating of the app | Average rating of the app. | 应用的平均评分。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.1.rating.rating_type` | the type of the rating can take the following values: Max5 | Rating scale used; Max5 denotes a 0-5 scale. | 所用评分量表;Max5 表示 0 至 5 分制。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.1.rating.value` | the value of the rating | The rating value. | 评分数值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.1.rating.votes_count` | the amount of feedback in this case, the value will be null | Number of ratings contributing to the value. | 参与构成该评分的评价数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.1.rating.rating_max` | the maximum value for a rating_type the maximum value for Max5 is 5 | Maximum possible value for the rating scale. | 该评分量表的最大可能值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.1.is_free` | indicates whether the app is free | Whether the app is free; the nested fields carry its pricing details when it is not. | 应用是否免费;非免费时其内嵌字段承载定价详情。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.1.is_free.current` | current price refers to the current price indicated in the element | Current price shown in the listing. | Listing 中显示的当前价格。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.1.is_free.regular` | regular price refers to the regular price indicated in the element | Regular (non-promotional) price shown in the listing. | Listing 中显示的常规(非促销)价格。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.1.is_free.max_value` | the maximum price refers to the maximum price indicated in the element | Maximum price shown in the listing. | Listing 中显示的最高价格。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.1.is_free.currency` | currency of the listed price ISO code of the currency applied to the price | ISO currency code applied to the listed price. | Listing 价格所用的 ISO 货币代码。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.1.is_free.is_price_range` | price is provided as a range indicates whether a price is provided in a range | Whether the price is given as a range rather than a single value. | 价格是否以区间而非单一数值给出。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.1.is_free.displayed_price` | price string in the result raw price string as provided in the result | Raw price string exactly as shown in the listing. | Listing 中原样展示的价格字符串。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.1.developer` | name of the app developer | Name of the app's developer. | 应用开发者的名称。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.intersection_result.1.developer_url` | URL to the developer page on Google Play | URL of the developer's store page. | 开发者商店页的 URL。 |

## post_dataforseo_dataforseo_labs_google_bulk_app_metrics_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | This endpoint will provide you with ranking metrics for up to 1000 Google Play applications. | Returns Google Play SERP ranking metrics for a batch of target apps in one request, letting you compare how multiple apps perform across their ranking keywords within one location and language. | 单次请求为一批目标应用返回 Google Play SERP 排名指标,便于在同一地区、语言下横向对比多个应用在其排名关键词上的表现。 |
| `req.app_ids` | ids of the app required field IDs of the mobile applications on Google Play; you can find the ID in the URL of every app listed on Google Play; example: in the URL https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=org.telegram.messenger the id is org.telegram.messenger; the maximum number of IDs you can specify in this field is 1000 | IDs of the target apps whose keyword overlap you want; take each ID from the app's App Store URL and supply them as an object of indexed entries. | 需求取关键词交集的目标应用 ID;每个 ID 取自 App Store 页 URL,以带序号条目的对象形式提供。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of the location required field if you don’t specify location_code Note: it is required to specify either location_name or location_code you can receive the list of available locations with their location_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages; Note: this endpoint currently supports the US location only; example: United States | Geographic target given by its full location name; supply either this or location_code. Look up valid names via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以完整地区名称指定的地理目标;与 location_code 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | location code required field if you don’t specify location_name Note: it is required to specify either location_name or location_code you can receive the list of available locations with their location_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages; Note: this endpoint currently supports the US location only; example: 2840 | Geographic target given by its numeric location code; supply either this or location_name. Look up valid codes via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以数字地区代码指定的地理目标;与 location_name 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效代码。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of the language required field if you don’t specify language_code Note: it is required to specify either language_name or language_code you can receive the list of available languages with their language_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages; Note: this endpoint currently supports the English language only; example: English | Target language given by its full name; supply either this or language_code. Look up valid names via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以完整名称指定的目标语言;与 language_code 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | language code required field if you don’t specify language_name Note: it is required to specify either language_name or language_code you can receive the list of available languages with their language_code by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages; Note: this endpoint currently supports the English language only example: en | Target language given by its short code; supply either this or language_name. Look up valid codes via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以简码指定的目标语言;与 language_name 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效代码。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Free-form label you attach to the task so you can match it to its result later; echoed back in the response data object. | 你为任务附加的自定义标签,便于事后将任务与结果对应;会在响应的 data 对象中原样回传。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version that produced this response. | 生成本响应的 API 版本。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall status code for the response; inspect it before reading results and handle non-success codes accordingly. | 本响应的总体状态码;读取结果前应先检查,并对非成功状态码做相应处理。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message that accompanies the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Wall-clock time spent producing the response, in seconds. | 生成响应所耗费的时间,单位为秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total charge for all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本响应中所有任务的合计费用,单位为美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task objects in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中任务对象的数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | Number of tasks in the tasks array that returned an error. | tasks 数组中以错误返回的任务数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task objects, one per task in the request batch. | 任务对象列表,请求批次中每个任务对应一项。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique task identifier in UUID format. | 任务在系统中的唯一标识,采用 UUID 格式。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of the response codes here | Overall status code for the response; inspect it before reading results and handle non-success codes accordingly. | 本响应的总体状态码;读取结果前应先检查,并对非成功状态码做相应处理。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message that accompanies the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Wall-clock time spent producing the response, in seconds. | 生成响应所耗费的时间,单位为秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Total charge for all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本响应中所有任务的合计费用,单位为美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of elements in this task's result array. | 本任务 result 数组中的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments of the endpoint that produced the task. | 生成该任务的接口 URL 路径分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters supplied in the request. | 对请求中所传参数的回传。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | List of all fields available for the filters and order_by parameters, grouped by the endpoint they apply to. | 可用于 filters 与 order_by 参数的全部字段列表,按其适用的接口分组。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.app_id` | id of the app in a POST array | App store ID; in results, the app this record describes. | 应用商店 ID;在结果中为该记录所描述的应用。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.location_code` | location code in a POST array | Location code echoed from the request; null when no data applies. | 从请求回传的地区代码;无对应数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.language_code` | language code in a POST array | Language code echoed from the request; null when no data applies. | 从请求回传的语言代码;无对应数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.total_count` | total amount of results in our database relevant to your request | Total number of matching records in the database for this request, which may exceed the number returned. | 数据库中匹配本请求的记录总数,可能多于实际返回的条数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items_count` | the number of results returned in the items array | Number of records returned in this items array. | 本 items 数组中返回的记录数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items` | contains data related to the ranking app metrics of the specified application | Returned records carrying the core data of this endpoint. | 返回的记录,承载本接口的核心数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.app_id` | id of the app in a POST array | App store ID; in results, the app this record describes. | 应用商店 ID;在结果中为该记录所描述的应用。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.metrics` | metrics for the ranking keywords of the app ranking data relevant to the keywords that the provided application ranks for on Google Play | Ranking and traffic metrics for the target, grouped by SERP result type. | 目标的排名与流量指标,按 SERP 结果类型分组。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.metrics.google_play_search_organic` | ranking data from Google Play organic search | Ranking data from Google Play organic search. | 来自 Google Play 自然搜索的排名数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.metrics.google_play_search_organic.pos_1` | number of SERPs where the app ranks #1 in organic results | Count of SERPs where the entity ranks #1. | 实体排名第 1 的 SERP 数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.metrics.google_play_search_organic.pos_2_3` | number of SERPs where the app ranks #2-3 in organic results | Count of SERPs where the entity ranks in positions 2-3. | 实体排名第 2 至 3 位的 SERP 数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.metrics.google_play_search_organic.pos_4_10` | number of SERPs where the app ranks #4-10 in organic results | Count of SERPs where the entity ranks in positions 4-10. | 实体排名第 4 至 10 位的 SERP 数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.metrics.google_play_search_organic.pos_11_100` | number of SERPs where the app ranks #11-100 in organic results | Count of SERPs where the entity ranks in positions 11-100. | 实体排名第 11 至 100 位的 SERP 数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.metrics.google_play_search_organic.count` | total count of organic SERPs that contain the app | Total count of SERPs of this type that contain the entity. | 包含该实体的此类 SERP 总数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.metrics.google_play_search_organic.search_volume` | total search volume of the app’s ranking keywords in Google Play organic SERP | Approximate average monthly search volume for the keyword. | 关键词的近似月均搜索量。 |

| `(operation)` | This endpoint will provide you with estimated monthly traffic volumes for up to 1,000 domains, subdomains, or webpages. Along with organic search traffic estimations, you will also get separate values for paid search, featured snippet, and local pack results. | Returns estimated monthly Google search traffic for a batch of target domains, broken down by SERP result type, so you can compare traffic across many domains in one request. | 为一批目标域名返回 Google 搜索的估算月度流量,并按 SERP 结果类型拆分,便于单次请求横向比较多个域名的流量。 |
| `req.targets` | target domains, subdomains, and webpages required field you can specify domains, subdomains, and webpages in this field; domains and subdomains should be specified without https:// and www.; pages should be specified with absolute URL, including https:// and www.; you can set up to 1000 domains, subdomains or webpages | Target domains and subdomains to estimate traffic for in one batch; specify each without https:// and www. | 需批量估算流量的目标域名与子域名;每项指定时均不带 https:// 与 www.。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of the location if you use this field, you don’t have to specify location_code you can receive the list of available locations with their location_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages ignore this field to get the results for all available locations example: United Kingdom | Geographic target given by its full location name; supply either this or location_code. Look up valid names via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以完整地区名称指定的地理目标;与 location_code 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效名称。 |
